 The full moon of the Shukla Paksha of Ashchin month is celebrated as Sharad Purnima
 sharad poornima ko kojogaar poornima vrath or raas poornima bhi kaha jaataa he
 On this day, recitation of Laxmistotra, Srisukta should be done
 is vidhi se kojagar vrath karne se mata lakshmi ati prasann hoti hai tathaa dhan-dhaany, maan-pratishtha aadi sabhisukh pradaanakrti hai
 Sharad Purnima fasting method- On the full moon day, in the morning one should worship the presiding deity
 - indra or mahalakshmi ji kaa pujan karke ghi ke deepak jalaakar uski gandh pushp aadi se puja kerani chahie
 - Brahmins should have kheer food and offer alms to Dakshina
 - lakshmi prapti ke liye is vrath ko vishesh rup se kiya jaataa he
 On this day, the wealth and wealth of those who awakened are increased
 - raat ko chandramaa ko arghya dene ke baad hi bhojan karnaa chahie
 - There is a law of offering Kheer in the temple
 aisa mana jaataa he ki is din chand kii chandani se amrit barasata he
 According to the importance of Sharad Purnima, if the rituals are performed on this day, then it is definitely successful
 tisare pahar is din vrath kar haathiyon kii aarti karne par utam fal milte he
 It is believed that Lord Krishna composed Maharas with the gopis on this day
 is din chandramaa ki kirnon se amrit varsha hone kii kivdanti prasiddh he
 For this reason, by making kheer on this day and keeping it in the moonlight overnight, there is a method of eating in the morning on the next day
 sharad poornima vrath kathakthanusaar ek sahuukaar kii do betiyaan thi or donon poornima kaa vrath rakhti thi
 The elder daughter duly completed the fast and the younger left the fast incomplete
 falswaroop choti ladki ke bachche janm lete hi mar jate the
 Once the virtuous touch of the elder girl made her child come alive and from that day onwards, this fast started to be celebrated in full
 is din mata mahalakshmi ji kii puja kii jaati he
 It is believed that by fasting on this day, all wishes are fulfilled
 kyon lagaaya jaataa he kheer kaa bhoga?is din vrath rakh kar vidhividhan se lakshminarayan kaa pujan karen or raat main kheer banaakar use raat main aasmaan ke neeche rakh den taaki chandramaa kii chandani kaa prakaash kheer par pade
 On the second day, take a bath in the morning and offer Kheer in your home's temple to at least 3 Brahmins as Kheer Prasad and then distribute the Kheer Prasad to your family
 is prasad ko grahan karne se anek prakaar ke rogon se chhutkaaraa miltaa he
 What science says 
 
 sharad poornima kii raat chandramaa hamaari dharti ke bahut kareeb hota he
 Therefore the chemical elements present in the light of the moon fall directly on the earth
 khaane-pine kii chijen khule aasmaan ke neeche rakhane se chandramaa kii kirne sidhe un par padati he jisase vishesh poshak tatv khaadya padaarthon main mil jate hai jo hamaari sehat ke liye anukool hote hai

 gujarat ke paanch stesan- gandhidam, jamnagar, surat, rajkot or ankleshwar sheersh 10 main shaamil hai
 The dirtiest stations by ranking include Madhubani, Ballia, Bakhtiyarpur, Raichur, Shahganj, Janghai, Anugraha Narayan, Sugauli, Ara and Pratapgarh with five of the dirtiest stations - Madhubani, Bakhtiyarpur, Anugraha Narayan, Sagouli and Ara - in Bihar

 He said that information of a person can be misused even if there is a situation of law and order or there is a disaster in public safety and public emergency
